line-height: 150%;\">one underrated Western movie with <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>kick ass dialogues. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It&nbsp;is a&nbsp;very intense, interesting character study of a famous lawman Wyatt Earp. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is common now for modern Hollywood characters to ask the other guy \u201c Who the fuck do you think you are, Wyatt Earp?\u201d&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; The melody of the background score grows on you after several viewings. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u201c There aint no humor in here: this is a serious story!\u201d , so will shout movie critics \u2014but people who can read between the lines know the humor inherent woven in it. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wyatt Berry Stapp Earp</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"> ( 1848 \u2013 1929) in real life was an American gambler, investor, and Marshall who served in several old West town. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He was also at different times a miner, farmer, bouncer, bar keeper and boxing referee. However, he was never a cowboy. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He is most well known for his part in the <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Gunfight at OK Corral. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>gunfight would define the rest of his life. Earp's modern-day reputation is that of \u201c The toughest and deadliest gunman of the old West\"</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>  </o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p><em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The movie starts with young Wyatt preparing to run away from home and join the Union army like his brothers Virgil and James. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>His father Gene Hackman in a cameo role, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>stops him. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>While Wyatt wants the same adventure he feels his brothers are experiencing, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>his father knows the horrors and truth about war . Later, James and Virgil return home both exhausted and beat up from serving in the army. Their father has put on his traveling shoes and announces that the family will be moving West where opportunity knocks. Wyatt finally ends up as a lawman and along with his brothers, clean up <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Dodge City.</span></span></em></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #111111; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em>Kicked out for being too tough Wyatt travels to Fort Griffin, Texas, where he meets and befriends Doc Holliday (Dennis Quaid), a former dentist, frequent gambler, occasional outlaw, and suffering from severe tuberculosis. Two demanding women also enter widower Wyatt's life,&nbsp; the&nbsp;prostitute Mattie (Mare Winningham) and stage performer Josie (Joanna Going) from San Fransico.</em></span></div>\n<em>  </em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #111111; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em>Another stint in Dodge City follows before the Earps relocate to Tombstone, Arizona. &nbsp;Wyatt and his brothers Virgil and Morgan manage to antagonize the local cattle rustlers known as The Cowboys, including members of the Clanton, Claiborne, and McLaury clans. </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: #111111; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em>The escalating tension climaxes with the famous Gunfight at the O.K. Corral, in which the Earp brothers helped by Holliday kill them three Cowboys. The Earps are subsequently targeted with retribution attacks, with Morgan killed and Virgil maimed. Wyatt sets off to kill all remaining Cowboys, before continuing his life out west in the company of Josie.</em></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Some kick-ass dialogues:-- ( with the Yank drawl )</span></strong></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Stop talking and start shooting. <o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"> You've raised your hand to me for the last time!  <br style=\"mso-special-character: line-break;\" /> <o:p></o:p></span></em></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></em></span></div>\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">  </span></em><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Put that gun down, Kate. Their 200 year old ancestral tharavadu house , which they sold -- is now converted to a church.</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XsyYkJTSBG8/TuHAWJQg53I/AAAAAAAAJl0/yv2b35Fr1-s/s1600/l.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XsyYkJTSBG8/TuHAWJQg53I/AAAAAAAAJl0/yv2b35Fr1-s/s1600/l.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Above is my elder son, who is now a computer engineer. Real Amul baby he was.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; , serif;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-V3IDARTwObs/TuHAxvJ2D_I/AAAAAAAAJl8/hW1A7NXlKII/s1600/a.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"416\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-V3IDARTwObs/TuHAxvJ2D_I/AAAAAAAAJl8/hW1A7NXlKII/s640/a.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is my wife's school ( Auxilium convent , Mumbai ) gang--who came to visit my container ship at Mumbai. I guess they believed that I was the Captain of a huge ship - only after seeing the Abandon ship Muster list posted on the notice board. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To be frank I used to look young for my age. When this ship went to USA in 1984, the US Coast Guard came to my cabin, started whispering KHUSSR PHUSSSR to each other, and then they went to the alleyway for further secret discussions and parleys . &nbsp;Finally they came back inside and wanted to see my passport and Seaman's book. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I asked them- why?&nbsp; &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Chief of this USCG six man boarding party said \" Captain don't you think you are too young to cross the Atlantic!\".&nbsp; So I told them off&nbsp; \"&nbsp; This is my third ship as Captain, and I have crossed two larger oceans Pacific and Indian . And my wife is in the bedroom-- I am NOT the Captain's son . You are excused, &nbsp;as while entering New York today, the Pilot came on bridge and&nbsp;tells my Cadet - GOOD MORNING CAPTAIN&nbsp; - and gives him the newspaper!\"</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JyNlSf0h8uQ/TuHCY2P7LiI/AAAAAAAAJmE/sK6PAMPyFC4/s1600/124.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"368\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JyNlSf0h8uQ/TuHCY2P7LiI/AAAAAAAAJmE/sK6PAMPyFC4/s640/124.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vzPGpjhVSPM/TuHDDdtSDtI/AAAAAAAAJmM/V8X0AO7dWs8/s1600/107.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vzPGpjhVSPM/TuHDDdtSDtI/AAAAAAAAJmM/V8X0AO7dWs8/s640/107.jpg\" width=\"233\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; Above picture is me and mE wife-- at our honeymoon.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 200%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XP2VIBM3XEA/TuHDhA1WxiI/AAAAAAAAJmk/43_PnQkLM1I/s1600/n.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"277\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XP2VIBM3XEA/TuHDhA1WxiI/AAAAAAAAJmk/43_PnQkLM1I/s400/n.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAbove picture is me as a young Second Mate. The cycle was used by the Duty officer for his rounds. Taking a round of that (VLCC tanker) &nbsp;on deck meant walking nearly ONE KILOMETER.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 200%;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-f4PbKOWSL3k/TuHD9q-jNdI/AAAAAAAAJms/NSPTh7-p1gY/s1600/f.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\nThat is me as a Chief officer with 3 stripes. \" Third Mate-- call me when it is time to do COW ( Crude oil wash )!\" </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Xh5aJ9nPbSQ/TuHRP7duEzI/AAAAAAAAJos/bns7-ZKsrD8/s1600/w.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Xh5aJ9nPbSQ/TuHRP7duEzI/AAAAAAAAJos/bns7-ZKsrD8/s1600/w.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\nI allow my Cadets to run free.&nbsp; I believe if young COLTS must win the jackpot later in life, you cant crush their spirits early in life.&nbsp; I remember this particular cadet came to for advise. He had always ignored his girlfriend who kept throwing herself at him. Now he is feeling a wee bit bad for she has just won \"MISS INDIA contest!\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-F09bZA0-34g/TuHF0diQonI/AAAAAAAAJnE/tsRxn0DnuDo/s1600/p.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-F09bZA0-34g/TuHF0diQonI/AAAAAAAAJnE/tsRxn0DnuDo/s640/p.jpg\" width=\"634\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dJLpFVjrzOg/TuHF7v7OLnI/AAAAAAAAJnM/aPcXuVaQVJw/s1600/e.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dJLpFVjrzOg/TuHF7v7OLnI/AAAAAAAAJnM/aPcXuVaQVJw/s640/e.jpg\" width=\"523\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWhen my wife first sailed with me in 1983, she cornered me one day. <br />\n<br />\nShe demanded \" <em><span style=\"color: blue;\">I want to know how you earn your wages. You do nothing throughout the day. You wake up at 9 AM, by the time&nbsp;you sit on your desk it is 10 AM.&nbsp; Between 10 and 10:45 whoever grabs&nbsp; your signature , gets it.&nbsp; The Purser comes at 1046, and you tell him --sorry it is my beer time.&nbsp; Then you have your lunch and go to sleep.&nbsp; At 4:30PM after tea, you go down and play TT and bullshit around playing TEEN PATTHI .&nbsp; Then you take a bath, have a beer and go for dinner.&nbsp; Then you write your night orders after having some discussions with the Chief officer and Chief Engineer on bridge and come down to watch&nbsp;a movie. Then you go to sleep . There goes another day--</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"><strong>How do you earn your wages?\"</strong></span> <br />\n<br />\nI replied \" Patience baby!&nbsp; Captain is meant to command and not to work.&nbsp; He will work only when warranted -- this is the way the cookie crumbles at sea!\"<br />\n<br />\nThen my non ice class ship had to load cargo at a port . Fantastic freight cargo was waiting in a pack ice bound port.&nbsp; All ice-class ships had got stuck, damaged their bows and propeller .&nbsp; The ice breakers were rescuing only stuck ships--&nbsp; and if you get stuck in pack ice, your turn could come 3 weeks later!\"<br />\n<br />\nFor three days I was on the bridge doing ice navigation.&nbsp; Cannot come down for a crap or even to brush my teeth.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nYou get stuck , then you have to reverse engines, putting your propeller in danger. You over speed or hit OLD HARD white ice, you bows can be kissed good bye.<br />\n<br />\nMy wife used to bring my toothpaste on bridge and to give me a neck massage. Finally when we reached the ice bound port everybody were surprised-- as my ship was NOT ice class.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eTvZUe2spoM/TuR9hDaOnrI/AAAAAAAAJx4/LHGahBkz3u4/s1600/55.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"425\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eTvZUe2spoM/TuR9hDaOnrI/AAAAAAAAJx4/LHGahBkz3u4/s640/55.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nI went down to sleep after arrival formalities, tossing around -- my body supercharged with adrenaline . <br />\n<br />\nMy wife whispered in mE ear \" Now I now know how you earn your wages!\"<br />\n<br />\nThere are many \"hard working\" Captains at sea.&nbsp; Almost all of them are incompetent-- they need to prove their worth to their crew -- by working hard, or sleeping on the bridge / CCR sofa . The Captains job is to provide a safe roof over the heads of his crew ! <br />\n<br />\nI have been lucky-- nearly 3 decades in command--- never damaged my ship even once, even a berthing bump on a ill fendered jetty, after more than a thousand berthings &nbsp;!-- luck plays a major factor here.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oJ1Wj08g26Y/TuHJrY9W7FI/AAAAAAAAJnU/q0AcjIhUTK4/s1600/h.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"484\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oJ1Wj08g26Y/TuHJrY9W7FI/AAAAAAAAJnU/q0AcjIhUTK4/s640/h.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThat is me and my ship mates -- painting a Venezuela beach RED . I am the guy in black shorts.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Gfmj_zIX6dQ/TuHKLM2dwaI/AAAAAAAAJnc/pZVwF59iHMM/s1600/g.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Why?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Damaged connection between pick-up and tachometer unit<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Pick up is not connected to turbocharger.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Turbocharger need to be cleaned/overhauled.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Pick up for tachometer is wrongly adjusted.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n201.The lubricating oil on the exhaust side of the turbine blower gets very dirty after only a few hours in service. What can the reason be?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Exhaust gas leaking into the oil chamber.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Wrong type of oil used.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Lubricating oil is mixed with salt water<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Worn out bearing turbine side<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n202.After water-washing the turbocharger exhaust side, the blower starts to vibrate. What has happened?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Water drain for washing system is clogged.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Foundation bolts for the blower unit are loose<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC The rotor blades are damaged or the blades are not properly cleaned<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Inlet filter partly clogged.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n203.The blower's air delivery is not sufficient. What is the cause?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Air temperature in engine room too high.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Dirty scavenge duct.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Clogged air inlet filter.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Cooling water temperature too high<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n204.Why is it important to slow down the main engine RPM while water-washing the turbocharger?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA To protect the bearings.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB To protect the exhaustgas economizer.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC To protect the blower side.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Not to damage the rotor blades.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n205.Some engine manufacturers recommend that washing of the compressor side is not carried out. Is this due to:<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Greasy sludge from the compressor sticking between the fins in the air coolers, necessitating extra cleaning of these.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Large volumes of water being carried over into the cylinders of the engine.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC The nozzle ring becoming corroded<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD The thermal shock exhibited by the vanes.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n206.What is the meaning of the term \"valve clearance\"?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA The clearance between the rocker arm and valve pushrod.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB The clearance between valve spindle disc and seat.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC The clearance between the rocker arm and camshaft pushrod.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD The clearance between the rocker arm and valve pushrod in either warm or cold state.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n207.The meaning of lapping a valve and valve seat is:.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Adjust the overlapping of the inlet and exhaust valves.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Grind the valve against the valve seat to obtain a uniform sealing surface.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Machining the valve in a lathe machine.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Repair by welding.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n208.Some 4-stroke engines are fitted with a rotorcap on the cylinder head valves. For what reason?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Rotate the inlet valve during operation.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Distribute the exhaust gas or the air inlet better to improve combustion.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Improve the scaling surface function, increase the service time of the exhaust valve in the engine<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD To prevent the valve spindle from sticking..<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n209.When overhauling the cylinder covers on a modern 4-stroke engine, is it important not to interchange inlet and exhaust valves?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA Not so important.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB Important due to different material and working conditions.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC Can be changed<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>if same size.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD Important due to different type size valve guide.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n210.What is the purpose of the cylinder head safety valve?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA To relieve excessive high pressure in the cylinder to protect the engine from being damaged.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB To adjust the cylinder pressure to a safe working pressure.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC A valve for safety stop (emergency) of the engine.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD For indication of engine being overloaded.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n211.Most of the engine makers recommend to change the cylinder head gaskets each time a piston overhaul is carried out. Why?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA To obtain a proper sealing and correct distance between piston and cover in TDC position.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB To increase the consumption of parts so they can make more money.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC To avoid heat transfer to the cylinder head.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nD To be granted a proper sealing with a new gasket.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n212.Some 4-stroke engines are equipped with cooled fuel valves. Why is it so important to keep the coolant's temperature correct?<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nA For cooling only.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nB For preheating only<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\nC To avoid overheating the fuel nozzle<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Status: Committee Hearings Held.<br />\n<hr />\n<b><a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/\" name=\"summary\">SUMMARY AS OF:</a></b><br />\n10/26/2011--Introduced.<br />\n<br />\nStop Online Piracy Act - Authorizes the Attorney General (AG) to seek a court order against a U.S.-directed foreign Internet site committing or facilitating online piracy to require the owner, operator, or domain name registrant, or the site or domain name itself if such persons are unable to be found, to cease and desist further activities constituting specified intellectual property offenses under the federal criminal code including criminal copyright infringement, unauthorized fixation and trafficking of sound recordings or videos of live musical performances, the recording of exhibited motion pictures, or trafficking in counterfeit labels, goods, or services.<br />\n<br />\nSets forth an additional two-step process that allows an intellectual property right holder harmed by a U.S.-directed site dedicated to infringement, or a site promoted or used for infringement under certain circumstances, to first provide a written notification identifying the site to related payment network providers and Internet advertising services requiring such entities to forward the notification and suspend their services to such an identified site unless the site's owner, operator, or domain name registrant, upon receiving the forwarded notification, provides a counter notification explaining that it is not dedicated to engaging in specified violations. Authorizes the right holder to then commence an action for limited injunctive relief against the owner, operator, or domain name registrant, or against the site or domain name itself if such persons are unable to be found, if: (1) such a counter notification is provided (and, if it is a foreign site, includes consent to U.S. jurisdiction to adjudicate whether the site is dedicated to such violations), or (2) a payment network provider or Internet advertising service fails to suspend its services in the absence of such a counter notification. <br />\nRequires online service providers, Internet search engines, payment network providers, and Internet advertising services, upon receiving a copy of a court order relating to an AG action, to carry out certain preventative measures including withholding services from an infringing site or preventing users located in the United States from accessing the infringing site. Requires payment network providers and Internet advertising services, upon receiving a copy of such an order relating to a right holder's action, to carry out similar preventative measures. <br />\nProvides immunity from liability for service providers, payment network providers, Internet advertising services, advertisers, Internet search engines, domain name registries, or domain name registrars that take actions required by this Act or otherwise voluntarily block access to or end financial affiliation with such sites.<br />\n<br />\nPermits such entities to stop or refuse services to certain sites that endanger public health by distributing prescription medication that is adulterated, misbranded, or without a valid prescription.<br />\n<br />\nExpands the offense of criminal copyright infringement to include public performances of: (1) copyrighted work by digital transmission, and (2) work intended for commercial dissemination by making it available on a computer network. Expands the criminal offenses of trafficking in inherently dangerous goods or services to include: (1) counterfeit drugs; and (2) goods or services falsely identified as meeting military standards or intended for use in a national security, law enforcement, or critical infrastructure application.<br />\n<br />\nIncreases the penalties for: (1) specified trade secret offenses intended to benefit a foreign government, instrumentality, or agent; and (2) various other intellectual property offenses as amended by this Act.<br />\n<br />\nDirects the U.S. Sentencing Commission to review, and if appropriate, amend related Federal Sentencing Guidelines.<br />\n<br />\nRequires the Secretary of State and Secretary of Commerce to appoint at least one intellectual property attache to be assigned to the U.S. embassy or diplomatic mission in a country in each geographic region covered by a Department of State regional bureau<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uBuCJbnR9Ww/TtuyOHiIfhI/AAAAAAAAJd0/OoYLl_YW5Y0/s1600/imagesCAI81Y9D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uBuCJbnR9Ww/TtuyOHiIfhI/AAAAAAAAJd0/OoYLl_YW5Y0/s1600/imagesCAI81Y9D.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe below video gives <span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">NAKED TRUTH</span> about the Rothchild Jewish bankers.
